<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="English">English</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mordor&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: English">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mordor&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mordor" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Mordor">Mordor</a>, a bleak realm ruled by the dark lord <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sauron" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Sauron">Sauron</a>, in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/J._R._R._Tolkien" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:J. R. R. Tolkien">J. R. R. Tolkien</a>'s fictional <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle-earth" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Middle-earth">Middle-earth</a>. Tolkien created the name in his constructed language <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sindarin" class="extiw" title="w:Sindarin">Sindarin</a></span></span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="sjn"><a href="/w/index.php?title=Appendix:Sindarin/mor&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Appendix:Sindarin/mor (page does not exist)">mor</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">dark, black</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="sjn"><a href="/w/index.php?title=Appendix:Sindarin/dor&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Appendix:Sindarin/dor (page does not exist)">dor</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">land</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mordor&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Received_Pronunciation" class="extiw" title="w:Received Pronunciation">Received Pronunciation</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:English_pronunciation" title="Appendix:English pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>: <span class="IPA">/ˈmɔːdɔː(ɹ)/</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/General_American" class="extiw" title="w:General American">General American</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:English_pronunciation" title="Appendix:English pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>: <span class="IPA">/ˈmɔɹdɔɹ/</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/New_Zealand_English_phonology" class="extiw" title="w:New Zealand English phonology">New Zealand</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:English_pronunciation" title="Appendix:English pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>: <span class="IPA">/ˈmoːdoː(ɹ)/</span></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Proper_noun">Proper noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mordor&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Proper noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">Mordor</strong>
</p>
<ol><li>An area of <a href="/wiki/peril" title="peril">peril</a>, <a href="/wiki/darkness" title="darkness">darkness</a>, or <a href="/wiki/evil" title="evil">evil</a>, which people fear to visit or explore.
<span class="HQToggle"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><dl><dd><i>One does not simply walk into <b>Mordor.</b></i></dd></dl>
<ul style="display: none;"><li><b>2007</b>, Paul F. M. Zahl, <i>Grace in Practice: A Theology of Everyday Life</i>, Wm. B. Eerdmans Publishing Co. (2007), <a href="/wiki/Special:BookSources/9780802828972" title="Special:BookSources/9780802828972">→ISBN</a>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://books.google.com/books?id=JjrzPYRIZHUC&amp;pg=PA94&amp;dq=%22a+mordor%22">page 94</a>:
<dl><dd>It is a “<b>Mordor</b>” sort of anthropology, dark rather than light, swampland rather than solid ground.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2007</b>, B. Erin Wylde, <i>Where Did I Go?</i>, <a href="/wiki/Special:BookSources/9781419673085" title="Special:BookSources/9781419673085">→ISBN</a>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://books.google.com/books?id=pJJXmURFYokC&amp;pg=PT56&amp;dq=%22the+mordor%22">page 100</a>:
<dl><dd>Nevertheless, this book is about the truth, the good and the bad, so I will tread into the forbidden territory, <i>the <b>Mordor</b> of motherhood</i>.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2012</b>, Zygmunt Miłoszewski, <i>A Grain of Truth: A Second Case for State Prosecutor Teodor Szacki</i>, Bitter Lemon Press (2012; original Polish book published 2011), <a href="/wiki/Special:BookSources/9781908524027" title="Special:BookSources/9781908524027">→ISBN</a>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://books.google.com/books?id=2OB3dExf1AEC&amp;lpg=PA290&amp;dq=%22this+mordor%22&amp;hl=de&amp;pg=PA290">page 290</a>:
<dl><dd>“OK, can we go back now?” asked their guide and expert on the underground, whose restless eyes implied that he was on the edge of panic. “I for one am not venturing a step further into this <b>Mordor</b>.”</dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="see-cites">For more quotations using this term, see <a href="/wiki/Citations:Mordor#English" title="Citations:Mordor">Citations:Mordor</a>.</span></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Polish">Polish</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mordor&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Polish">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation_2">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mordor&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:Polish_pronunciation" title="Appendix:Polish pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>: <span class="IPA">/ˈmɔr.dɔr/</span></li>
<li>Rhymes: <a href="/w/index.php?title=Rhymes:Polish/%C9%94rd%C9%94r&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Rhymes:Polish/ɔrdɔr (page does not exist)"><span class="IPA">-ɔrdɔr</span></a></li>
<li>Syllabification: <span class="Latn" lang="pl">Mor‧dor</span></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mordor&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="pl">Mordor</strong>&nbsp;<span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr>&nbsp;<abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#figurative" title="Appendix:Glossary">figuratively</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/Mordor#English" title="Mordor">Mordor</a></span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">area of peril, darkness, or evil</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Warsaw" class="extiw" title="w:Warsaw">Warsaw</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="/wiki/derogatory" title="derogatory">derogatory</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#colloquial" title="Appendix:Glossary">colloquial</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> office complexes on Domaniewska street in <a href="/w/index.php?title=S%C5%82u%C5%BCewiec&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Służewiec (page does not exist)">Służewiec</a>, a district of <a href="/wiki/Warsaw" title="Warsaw">Warsaw</a>
<span class="HQToggle"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2013</b>,  Nie sloik,  “Re: "Leming jedzie na Służewiec ściśnięty w pozyc...”, in  <cite>Forum Gazeta.pl</cite>‎<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://forum.gazeta.pl/forum/w,51,142683292,142683970,Re_Leming_jedzie_na_Sluzewiec_scisniety_w_pozyc.html">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="pl">A z resztą zgoda - dojazd zbiorkomem jest na Służewiec koszmarny. Nieoficjalna nazwa tej okolicy to od jakiegoś czasu <b>Mordor</b>.</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I agree with the others - mass transit to Służewiec is nightmarish. The unoffical name of this region has been for some time <b>Mordor</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mordor&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Usage notes">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>The relevant part of Służewiec is composed almost entirely of office buildings belonging to major <a href="/wiki/corporation" title="corporation">corporations</a> and <a href="/wiki/outsourcing" title="outsourcing">outsourcing</a> centers and suffers from poor transportation.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Declension">Declension</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mordor&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Declension">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="NavFrame inflection-table-noun" style="width: 19em">
<div class="NavHead" style="cursor: pointer;"><span class="NavToggle"><a role="button" tabindex="0">show ▼</a></span>Declension of <span class="Latn mention" lang="pl">Mordor</span></div>
<div class="NavContent" style="display: none;">
<table style="width: 19em; margin: 0;" class="wikitable inflection-table">

<tbody><tr>
<th style="width: 8em;">
</th>
<th scope="col">singular
</th></tr>
<tr>
<th title="mianownik (kto? co?)" scope="row">nominative
</th>
<td><span class="Latn" lang="pl"><a class="mw-selflink selflink">Mordor</a></span>
</td></tr>
<tr>
